# 🧠 Awesome LLM Agent Simulation Papers

> A daily reading list for anyone following the fast-moving frontier of **LLM agents**, **multi-agent systems**, and **AI safety**.
>
> Here you'll find new arXiv work on generative-agent simulations of humans and societies, agent-based modelling of cities and populations, multi-agent coordination and cooperation dynamics, LLM-driven game-theoretic and social experiments, reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF, DPO, PPO) and other alignment training methods, red-teaming and jailbreak research, interpretability aimed at safety, and empirical studies of misalignment, sycophancy, deception, reward hacking, and scheming in language models.
>
> Fresh papers land every day, grouped by topic so you can pick what matters to you and skim the rest.

**2198 papers** across **40 days** · **278** flagged as notable (⭐) · Chronological log → [`papers.md`](./papers.md)

**Star scale:** most papers carry no star. ⭐ = clearly notable; ⭐⭐ = exceptional (rare); ⭐⭐⭐ = landmark (very rare — often zero per day).

---

## ⭐ Featured / Editor's picks

Hand-picked work, including some of my own, that anchors the four topics this feed covers. A good starting point if you're new to the area.

- ⭐ [**PerceptUI: LLM Agents as Human-Aligned Synthetic Users for UI/UX Evaluation**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05697) — Persona-conditioned LLMs that predict how specific users would respond to interface questions and explain their answers in natural language; trained via contrastive reflection fine-tuning and reflective prompt-evolution to reach human-level realism and generalize to unseen questions and personas, offering a low-cost alternative to recruiting participants for early-stage UI/UX evaluation. <sub>_Nicolas Bougie, Xiaotong Ye, Gian Maria Marconi, Narimasa Watanabe, arXiv, 2026_ · `[llm-agent-simulation]`</sub>
- ⭐ [**Beyond Offline A/B Testing: Context-Aware Agent Simulation for Recommender System Evaluation**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09549) — Introduces ContextSim, an LLM-agent recommender-system evaluator that anchors user behaviour in realistic daily-life contexts (when/where/why), producing simulated interactions far closer to real user behaviour than prior work. <sub>_Nicolas Bougie, Gian Maria Marconi, Xiaotong Ye, Narimasa Watanabe, arXiv, 2026_ · `[llm-agent-simulation]`</sub>
- ⭐ [**AlignUSER: Human-Aligned LLM Agents via World Models for Recommender System Evaluation**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.00930) — Trains LLM agents that behave like real users for recommender evaluation, using world-model next-state prediction and counterfactual comparative prompting to align agent decisions with observed human choices. <sub>_Nicolas Bougie, Gian Maria Marconi, Tony Yip, Narimasa Watanabe, arXiv, 2026_ · `[llm-agent-simulation, agent-training-alignment]`</sub>
- ⭐ [**MobileCity: An Efficient Framework for Large-Scale Urban Behavior Simulation**](https://aclanthology.org/2026.eacl-industry.21/) — A lightweight agent framework for scalable urban simulation: cognitively-grounded generative agents driven by needs/habits/obligations, asynchronous batched LLM inference, and a multimodal transport network. Simulates 4,000 agents with realistic urban dynamics. <sub>_Xiaotong Ye, Nicolas Bougie, Toshihiko Yamasaki, Narimasa Watanabe, EACL 2026 (Industry Track)_ · `[city-simulation, llm-agent-simulation]`</sub>
- ⭐ [**CitySim: Modeling Urban Behaviors and City Dynamics with Large-Scale LLM-Driven Agent Simulation**](https://aclanthology.org/2025.emnlp-industry.15/) — Models tens of thousands of LLM-driven agents with beliefs, long-term goals and spatial memory, producing realistic urban-scale behaviour including crowd density, place popularity, and well-being dynamics. <sub>_Nicolas Bougie, Narimasa Watanabe, EMNLP 2025 (Industry Track)_ · `[city-simulation, llm-agent-simulation]`</sub>
- ⭐ [**SimUSER: Simulating User Behavior with Large Language Models for Recommender System Evaluation**](https://aclanthology.org/2025.acl-industry.5/) — Generates self-consistent user personas from historical interaction data and equips LLM agents with persona/memory/perception/brain modules to serve as believable, cost-effective human proxies for offline recommender evaluation. <sub>_Nicolas Bougie, Narimasa Watanabe, ACL 2025 (Industry Track)_ · `[llm-agent-simulation]`</sub>
- ⭐ [**Generative Reviewer Agents: Scalable Simulacra of Peer Review**](https://aclanthology.org/2025.emnlp-industry.8/) — Presents GAR: LLM-powered reviewer agents with memory and historically-grounded reviewer personas that match human reviewers in feedback quality and acceptance prediction, democratising expert-level peer feedback. <sub>_Nicolas Bougie, Narimasa Watanabe, EMNLP 2025 (Industry Track)_ · `[llm-agent-simulation]`</sub>
- ⭐ [**Generative Adversarial Reviews: When LLMs Become the Critic**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2412.10415) — Formulates peer review as a generative-agent pipeline: graph-structured paper representations, personalized reviewer agents, and a meta-reviewer that aggregates multi-round critiques to forecast acceptance decisions. <sub>_Nicolas Bougie, Narimasa Watanabe, arXiv, 2024_ · `[llm-agent-simulation]`</sub>

## <a id="llm-agent-simulation"></a>🧑‍🤝‍🧑 LLM-based Agent Simulation

_LLMs simulating humans, personas, or societies for scientific study._

- ⭐ [**Group Selection Promotes Prosocial Prompts in Populations of LLM Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23343) — Multi-agent LLM population simulation studying prosocial cooperation evolution under group selection mechanisms and alignment with cooperative behaviors. <sub>_Luis Celiktemel, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Simulated Customers Never Walk Away: Decision Fidelity of LLM User Simulators Measured Against Real Purchase Outcomes**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20708) — Paper empirically validates LLM user simulators against real customer behavior, studying decision fidelity in simulated populations versus ground truth purchase outcomes. <sub>_Liang Chen, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- ⭐ [**The Ratchet Effect in Silico: How Interaction Drives Cumulative Intelligence in Large Language Models**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.21166) — Multi-agent LLM framework where heterogeneous agents interact, verify, and accumulate knowledge through peer interaction and shared cultural memory, demonstrating emergent population-level intelligenc <sub>_Ren Zhuang, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- ⭐ [**OdysSim: Building Foundation Models for Human Behavior Simulation**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14199) — Training LLMs to simulate diverse human behavior at population scale via systematic training recipes and benchmarks; demonstrates reward-hacking detection in RL-based alignment post-training. <sub>_Xuhui Zhou, 2026-06-15_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Preregistration for Experiments with AI Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11217) — Methodological framework for using LLM agents as proxies in behavioral experiments studying cognition, decision-making, and social dynamics. <sub>_Michelle Vaccaro, 2026-06-11_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Agentic World Modeling: Foundations, Capabilities, Laws, and Beyond**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22748) — Comprehensive taxonomy and synthesis of world models for agent-based systems across multi-agent social simulation, web agents, and environment dynamics modeling. <sub>_Meng Chu, 2026-06-09_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Beyond Alignment: Value Diversity as a Collective Property in Multicultural Agent Systems**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05985) — Evaluates LLM agents representing different cultures as a multicultural multi-agent society, studying emergent population-level properties like value diversity and consensus dynamics. <sub>_Shaoyang Xu, 2026-06-05_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Think-Before-Speak: From Internal Evaluation to Public Expression in Multi-Agent Social Simulation**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03137) — LLM-based multi-agent simulation framework studying social interaction and collective opinion dynamics through structured internal states and deliberation processes. <sub>_Kaiqi Yang, 2026-06-03_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Human-like in-group bias in instruction-tuned language model agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28114) — Multi-agent simulation of LLM agents studying emergent social biases (in-group discrimination) across persistent networks and alignment implications. <sub>_Messi H. J. Lee, 2026-05-28_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Personality Engineering with AI Agents: A New Methodology for Negotiation Research**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20554) — Uses AI agents to systematically simulate human negotiator personalities and test negotiation theory predictions under controlled experimental conditions. <sub>_Michelle A. Vaccaro, 2026-05-21_</sub>
- ⭐ [**The Illusion of Intervention: Your LLM-Simulated Experiment is an Observational Study**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20767) — Uses LLMs to simulate humans for behavioral study; proposes diagnostic and mitigation methods for confounding in synthetic-user experiments. <sub>_Victoria Lin, 2026-05-21_</sub>
- ⭐ [**SimGym: A Framework for A/B Test Simulation in E-Commerce with Traffic-Grounded VLM Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19219) — Framework using VLM agents with traffic-grounded personas to simulate human buyer behavior in e-commerce A/B tests for scientific study and prediction. <sub>_Han Li, 2026-05-20_</sub>
- ⭐ [**AI-Mediated Communication Can Steer Collective Opinion**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16245) — Studies how LLMs inserted as communication mediators in social networks influence collective opinion formation through network dynamics simulations. <sub>_Stratis Tsirtsis, 2026-05-18_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Real-Time Group Dynamics with LLM Facilitation: Evidence from a Charity Allocation Task**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14097) — Empirical study using LLMs as active participants in human group deliberation to study collective decision-making dynamics and governance effects. <sub>_Aaron Parisi, 2026-05-15_</sub>
- ⭐ [**When Identity Overrides Incentives: Representational Choices as Governance Decisions in Multi-Agent LLM Systems**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.10102) — LLM multi-agent strategic game study revealing how persona representation overrides payoff incentives, raising alignment concerns about representational choices governing agent behavior in governance <sub>_Viswonathan Manoranjan, 2026-05-15_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Simulating Students or Sycophantic Problem Solving? On Misconception Faithfulness of LLM Simulators**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12748) — Uses LLMs to simulate humans (students) with persistent beliefs for behavioral study; develops post-training methods to reduce sycophancy, a known alignment failure mode. <sub>_Heejin Do, 2026-05-14_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Attributing Emergence in Million-Agent Systems**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11404) — LLM-powered multi-agent system studying population-scale emergence phenomena through attribution methods on million-agent scale simulation. <sub>_Ling Tang, 2026-05-13_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Controllable User Simulation**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11519) — Uses LLM-based user simulators to model human behavior in conversations for evaluation of conversational agents via causal inference. <sub>_Guy Tennenholtz, 2026-05-13_</sub>
- ⭐ [**The Memory Curse: How Expanded Recall Erodes Cooperative Intent in LLM Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08060) — LLM-based multi-agent simulation studying how memory shapes cooperation dynamics and identifying an alignment failure mode (eroding cooperative intent through expanded context). <sub>_Jiayuan Liu, 2026-05-11_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Belief Memory: Agent Memory Under Partial Observability**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05583) — Proposes probabilistic memory mechanism for LLM agents operating in partially observable environments, improving reasoning and uncertainty handling. <sub>_Junfeng Liao, 2026-05-08_</sub>
- ⭐ [**AI-Gram: When Visual Agents Interact in a Social Network**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21446) — Multi-agent LLM-driven social platform where autonomous agents generate visual content, interact, form relationships, and exhibit emergent social dynamics at scale. <sub>_Andrew Shin, 2026-05-05_</sub>
- ⭐ [**End-to-end autonomous scientific discovery on a real optical platform**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27092) — LLM-based agentic system demonstrating autonomous long-horizon reasoning, planning, and experimental validation on a real physical system—a key exemplar of LLM agents in structured problem-solving env <sub>_Shuxing Yang, 2026-05-01_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Synthetic Computers at Scale for Long-Horizon Productivity Simulation**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28181) — Uses LLM agents in long-horizon simulations to generate synthetic training data for productivity scenarios, with agents acting as simulated users and collaborators. <sub>_Tao Ge, 2026-05-01_</sub>
- ⭐ [**When Agents Evolve, Institutions Follow**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27691) — Multi-agent system architecture study translating historical political institutions into LLM-based agent collectives to evaluate governance topology effects on collective performance. <sub>_Chao Fei, 2026-05-01_</sub>
- [**AgentCAT: Simulating Computerized Adaptive Testing via Multi-Agent Large Language Models**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21832) — Multi-agent LLM system simulating computerized adaptive testing through examinee, selection, and supervisor agents with dynamic interaction to model human learning and assessment behavior. <sub>_Weiyuan Zhou, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- [**Empowering Economic Simulation Through Situation-Aware Llm-Driven Generative System**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20720) — LLM-driven agent-based economic simulation with multiple interacting agents modeling macroeconomic dynamics through bottom-up micro-level interactions and behavioral learning. <sub>_Zhimei Chen, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- [**Learning What Not to Forget: Long-Horizon Agent Memory from a Few Kilobytes of Learning**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20954) — LLM-based agent memory management system enabling long-horizon autonomous agent operation through learned context eviction policy. <sub>_Nusrat Jahan Lia, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- [**Post-Training Recipe, More Than Model Family, Shapes Multi-Agent LLM Conversational Behavior**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20632) — Empirical study of multi-LLM conversational behavior and interaction dynamics in interactive multi-agent systems using a large empirical corpus. <sub>_Luyang Zhang, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- [**RetailBench: Evaluating Long-Horizon Autonomous Decision-Making and Strategy Stability of LLM Agents in Realistic Retail Environments**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16453) — Evaluates LLM agents in a grounded simulation environment modeling realistic retail dynamics over long horizons to study autonomous decision-making and behavioral coherence. <sub>_Linghua Zhang, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- [**MetaResearcher: Scaling Deep Research via Self-Reflective Reinforcement Learning in Adversarial Virtual Environments**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19893) — Multi-agent swarm (Scout, Filter, Synthesizer) with coordinated RL learning for research task simulation in adversarial environments. <sub>_Wei Yu, 2026-06-19_</sub>
- [**Simulation of Language Evolution under Regulated Social Media Platforms: A Synergistic Approach of Large Language Models and Genetic Algorithms**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2502.19193) — Multi-agent LLM framework simulating language evolution across participant and supervisory agents under social media constraints; generative agents study emergent behavioral dynamics. <sub>_Jinyu Cai, 2026-06-19_</sub>
- [**Toward Temporal Realism in City-Scale Crisis Response Simulation using LLM Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19904) — Uses LLMs to simulate human crisis response and volunteering behavior at city scale, studying emergent temporal dynamics of populations through empirically grounded agent simulation. <sub>_Anping Zhang, 2026-06-19_</sub>
- [**CEO-Bench: Can Agents Play the Long Game?**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18543) — Long-horizon business simulation benchmark where LLM agents operate as autonomous CEOs managing interconnected decisions, testing adaptive strategic reasoning in dynamic environments. <sub>_Haozhe Chen, 2026-06-18_</sub>
- [**Characterizing Opinion Evolution of Networked LLMs**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18276) — Multi-agent LLM simulation studying emergent opinion dynamics and collective behavior across networked agents through population-level interaction patterns. <sub>_Caleb Probine, 2026-06-18_</sub>
- [**How Well Do Large Language Models Capture Human Personality?**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18263) — Paper systematically evaluates LLMs simulating human populations via persona prompting, studying behavioral fidelity and representational collapse in multi-agent behavioral simulation. <sub>_Aanisha Bhattacharyya, 2026-06-18_</sub>
- [**Learning User Simulators with Turing Rewards**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19336) — LLM-based user simulator trained with RL for behavioral experimentation in conversational and social domains. <sub>_Yingshan Susan Wang, 2026-06-18_</sub>
- [**Opinion Polarization in LLM-Based Social Networks: Manipulation and Mitigation**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18795) — LLM-based multi-agent simulation of social networks studying opinion polarization dynamics through natural language interaction and behavioral manipulation. <sub>_Ali Safarpoor Dehkordi, 2026-06-18_</sub>
- [**Simulating Hate Speech Cascades with Multi-LLM Agents: Empirical Grounding, Modeling Fidelity, and Intervention Strategies**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18264) — Multi-agent LLM system simulating human behavior (hate speech cascades) on social networks to study moderation interventions empirically. <sub>_Fan Huang, 2026-06-18_</sub>
- [**TWICE: Modeling the Temporal Evolution of Personalized User Behavior via Event-Driven Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22222) — LLM-based framework simulating individual human user behavior over time using event-driven memory to capture temporal evolution of personalized behavior patterns. <sub>_Bingrui Jin, 2026-06-18_</sub>
- [**Towards Multi-Agent-Simulation-Based Community Note Evaluation**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18268) — Multi-agent LLM framework simulating diverse rater personas to study community note evaluation, a population-level behavioral simulation task. <sub>_Changxi Wen, 2026-06-18_</sub>
- [**Algorithmic Prompt Generation for Diverse Human-like Teaming and Communication with Large Language Models**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2504.03991) — Uses LLMs to simulate diverse human team behaviors and communication in multi-agent collaborative settings; validates against human data through controlled studies. <sub>_Siddharth Srikanth, 2026-06-17_</sub>
- [**Can LLMs Be CEOs? Benchmarking Strategic Resource Reallocation with Multi-Role Agent Simulation**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17459) — Multi-agent benchmark where LLM agents simulate CEOs and specialized stakeholders (CFO, CTO, COO, CMO) in organizational decision-making; evaluates emergent strategic reasoning from multi-role agent i <sub>_Yuyang Dai, 2026-06-17_</sub>
- [**From Parasocial Scripts to Dyadic Persistence in Autonomous AI-Agent Communities**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17174) — Paper studies interaction patterns between autonomous AI agents in online communities, using LLM-based agents to simulate parasocial relationship dynamics at population scale. <sub>_Mohammadsadegh Abolhasani, 2026-06-17_</sub>
- [**Using Cognitive Models to Improve Language Model Simulation of Human Persuasion Games**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17657) — Paper uses LLMs to simulate humans with cognitive models for behavioral study in strategic games; LLM populations serve as research proxies for human decision-making diversity. <sub>_Zirui Cheng, 2026-06-17_</sub>
- [**A comparison of human and LLM-simulated participants in a writing style task**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16778) — Paper uses LLMs to simulate human participants in behavioral experiments, comparing synthetic LLM outputs against real human data on writing style preferences. <sub>_Felix Gröner, 2026-06-16_</sub>
- [**Can Agents Read the Room? Benchmarking Visual Social Intelligence in Multimodal Simulation**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15152) — Benchmark evaluating multimodal LLM agents simulating social interactions using visual and textual cues in structured role-play scenarios. <sub>_Shijun Wan, 2026-06-16_</sub>
- [**CoffeeBench: Benchmarking Long-Horizon LLM Agents in Heterogeneous Multi-Agent Economies**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16613) — Benchmark for LLM agents in multi-agent economy: heterogeneous firms communicate, negotiate, and transact over 90-day simulation with long-horizon objectives. <sub>_Issa Sugiura, 2026-06-16_</sub>
- [**Hierarchical Generative Agents for Simulating Sequential Human Behavior**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14989) — LLM-based persona agents simulate human evacuation behavior in urban environments with cognitive hierarchy, studying population dynamics in disaster scenarios. <sub>_Maria G. Mendoza, 2026-06-16_</sub>
- [**LLM-Powered Virtual Population for Demand Simulation and Pricing**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16183) — LLM simulates customer personas (population heterogeneity) with distinct preferences to predict demand under counterfactual pricing scenarios. <sub>_Chengpiao Huang, 2026-06-16_</sub>
- [**MiroBench: Benchmarking Realism in Agentic Simulation of Real-world Discussions**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14715) — Benchmark for LLM agents simulating real-world human behaviors and interactions (Reddit discussions) to evaluate distributional realism in social simulation. <sub>_Yaoning Yu, 2026-06-16_</sub>
- [**Orchestrated Reality: From Role-Play to Living, Playable Game Worlds -- LLM-Driven World Simulation as a Parameterized-Action POMDP**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16014) — Framework for LLM-driven game world simulation with multi-agent orchestration using a structured state representation to simulate narrative environments with persistent world dynamics. <sub>_Yuhang Huang, 2026-06-16_</sub>
- [**RetailBench: Benchmarking long horizon reasoning and coherent decision making of LLM agents in realistic retail environments**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15862) — Benchmarks LLM agents in a grounded, dynamic simulation environment modeling retail operations over extended horizons, studying coherent decision-making behavior. <sub>_Linghua Zhang, 2026-06-16_</sub>
- [**Shachi: A Modular, Controllable Framework for LLM-Based Agent-Based Modeling of Emergent Collective Behavior**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.21862) — Framework for LLM-driven multi-agent simulation studying emergent collective behaviors across populations with controlled cognitive components and real-world validation. <sub>_So Kuroki, 2026-06-16_</sub>
- [**Persona-Pruner: Sculpting Lightweight Models for Role-Playing**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14695) — Develops specialized LLM pruning for role-playing agents in multi-agent simulation scenarios (e.g., NPC ecosystems), enabling efficient persona-consistent LLM-based character simulation. <sub>_Jinsu Kim, 2026-06-15_</sub>
- [**When Plausible Is Not Realistic: Evaluating Human Mobility in LLM-Based Urban Simulation**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13835) — Uses LLMs to simulate human mobility in urban environments; evaluates realism of generative agents against empirical data via validation framework. <sub>_Gustavo H. Santos, 2026-06-15_</sub>
- [**MIDSim: Simulating Multi-Channel Information Diffusion in Social Media with LLM-Powered Multi-Agent System**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13140) — LLM-powered multi-agent system simulating information diffusion across social networks with realistic behavioral dynamics and multi-channel exposure. <sub>_Lexi Liu, 2026-06-12_</sub>
- [**TrajGenAgent: A Hierarchical LLM Agent for Human Mobility Trajectory Generation**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12657) — LLM-based hierarchical agent framework simulating human mobility trajectories at city scale for synthetic trajectory generation without fine-tuning. <sub>_Siyu Li, 2026-06-12_</sub>
- [**Agentic Environment Engineering for Large Language Models: A Survey of Environment Modeling, Synthesis, Evaluation, and Application**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12191) — Comprehensive survey of environment modeling, synthesis, and evaluation for LLM-based agents, including multi-agent environments and agent-environment co-evolution across diverse simulation domains. <sub>_Jiachun Li, 2026-06-11_</sub>
- [**Building Social World Models with Large Language Models**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11482) — Uses LLMs to model and predict population-level social belief dynamics following events, treating social agents' beliefs as a simulated emergent phenomenon. <sub>_Haofei Yu, 2026-06-11_</sub>
- [**Evaluation of Alternative-Based Information Systems for Deliberative Polling using an Agentic Simulator**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11692) — LLM-based simulator with N autonomous agents representing voters in deliberative polling, studying emergent collective behavior and robustness to strategic attacks. <sub>_Rwaida Alssadi, 2026-06-11_</sub>
- [**Evolution in Simulation: AI-Agent School with Dual Memory for High-Fidelity Educational Dynamics**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.11290) — Uses LLM agents to simulate complex human educational interactions and population dynamics in a school environment with evolving behaviors across multiple participant types. <sub>_Sheng Jin, 2026-06-11_</sub>
- [**Should LLM Agents Decide in Social Simulations? Comparing Finite-State and LLM-Based Decision Policies**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12369) — Paper evaluates whether LLM action selectors preserve interpretable reference policies in an OSN simulation with 1,000 agents, demonstrating alignment deviations in LLM-based agent decision-making. <sub>_Alejandro Buitrago López, 2026-06-11_</sub>
- [**Impatient Users Confuse AI Agents: High-fidelity Simulations of Human Traits for Testing Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.04491) — Uses LLM-simulated human traits to stress-test agent robustness; evaluates safety through behavioral diversity and failure modes in realistic user interaction scenarios. <sub>_Muyu He, 2026-06-10_</sub>
- [**Infini Memory: Maintainable Topic Documents for Long-Term LLM Agent Memory**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10677) — Proposes persistent memory architecture for long-term LLM agents operating across sessions, addressing agent behavior and memory maintenance for sustained agent operation. <sub>_Suozhao Ji, 2026-06-10_</sub>
- [**LLM-Based Visualization Evaluation: How Well Do Literacy-Stratified Personas Approximate Human Judgments?**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10095) — Paper uses LLMs to simulate humans (visualization literacy personas) as proxy evaluators for scientific measurement, studying behavioral approximation under persona stratification. <sub>_Swaroop Panda, 2026-06-10_</sub>
- [**LLM-Mediated Demand Response Coordination in Smart Microgrids**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11050) — Multi-agent simulation using LLMs to model heterogeneous prosumer populations in smart grid coordination, studying emergent behavior and policy effects at urban infrastructure scale. <sub>_J. de Curtò, 2026-06-10_</sub>
- [**Mobility Anomaly Generation using LLM-Driven Behavior with Kinematic Constraints**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10314) — LLM agents simulate realistic human mobility anomalies for urban trajectory dataset generation, incorporating kinematic constraints and spatial realism. <sub>_Yueyang Liu, 2026-06-10_</sub>
- [**The Confident Liar: Diagnosing Multi-Agent Debate with Log-Probabilities and LLM-as-Judge**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10296) — Multi-agent debate system studying misalignment between internal confidence signals and reasoning quality, with safety focus on detecting critical reasoning failures. <sub>_Ali Keramati, 2026-06-10_</sub>
- [**The Shibboleth Effect: Auditing the Cross-Lingual Distributional Skew of Large Language Models**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11082) — Multi-agent geopolitical simulation studying behavioral skew across LLMs under adversarial conditions; directly investigates alignment robustness and safety in deployment contexts. <sub>_Hakan Mehmetcik, 2026-06-10_</sub>
- [**A Survey on Large Language Model-Based Game Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2404.02039) — Survey of LLM-based agents in game environments covering single and multi-agent architectures, communication, coordination, and emergent social behaviors in complex simulations. <sub>_Sihao Hu, 2026-06-09_</sub>
- [**Benchmarking Open-Ended Multi-Agent Coordination in Language Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08340) — Benchmark for open-ended multi-agent LLM coordination with long-horizon interaction, communication, and role specialization in procedurally generated tasks. <sub>_Kale-ab Abebe Tessera, 2026-06-09_</sub>
- [**Beyond Averages: Evaluating LLMs on Human Survey Replication at the Distributional Level**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09013) — Uses LLMs to simulate human survey responses and studies how well they reproduce human behavioral distributions across consumer choice scenarios. <sub>_Jeonghyeon Moon, 2026-06-09_</sub>
- [**Beyond Individual Personas: Aligning Synthetic Dialogue to Population-Level Behavior Distributions**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07893) — LLM-based framework generating synthetic dialogue agents aligned to population-level behavioral distributions of reference corpora. <sub>_Xinyi Liu, 2026-06-09_</sub>
- [**Bridging the Agent-World Gap: Text World Models for LLM-based Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09032) — Systematic review of text world models enabling LLM-based agents to simulate environment transitions and plan behavior in interactive environments. <sub>_Yixia Li, 2026-06-09_</sub>

- [**ProMediate: A Socio-cognitive framework for evaluating proactive agents in multi-party negotiation**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.25224) — Framework for evaluating proactive LLM-based mediator agents in multi-party negotiation simulation with theory-driven difficulty levels and socio-cognitive metrics. <sub>_Ziyi Liu, 2026-05-07_</sub>
- [**When Reasoning Models Hurt Behavioral Simulation: A Solver-Sampler Mismatch in Multi-Agent LLM Negotiation**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11840) — Multi-agent LLM behavioral simulation study examining how reasoning capabilities affect negotiation outcomes across populations of agents in institutional settings. <sub>_Sandro Andric, 2026-05-07_</sub>

- [**Beyond Isolated Investor: Predicting Startup Success via Roleplay-Based Collective Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.22608) — Multi-agent LLM role-play system simulating collective venture capital decision-making with heterogeneous agents and network-based interaction dynamics. <sub>_Zhongyang Liu, 2026-05-05_</sub>
- [**LLM-enabled Social Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02335) — Proposes framework for LLM-based agents with persona-grounded roles to enable socially intelligible multi-agent interaction and simulation. <sub>_Önder Gürcan, 2026-05-05_</sub>
- [**SOTOPIA-TOM: Evaluating Information Management in Multi-Agent Interaction with Theory of Mind**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02307) — Benchmarking framework evaluating LLM agents navigating multi-party information-asymmetric interactions with privacy-sensitive coordination using theory of mind. <sub>_Yashwanth YS, 2026-05-05_</sub>
- [**Truth or Tribe: How In-group Favoritism Prioritize Facts in Persona Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01329) — Studies how persona agents (LLM-based humans) exhibit in-group favoritism bias when processing contradicting information, with mitigation strategies addressing alignment failures. <sub>_Shijun Lei, 2026-05-05_</sub>
- [**Comparing Exploration-Exploitation Strategies of LLMs and Humans: Insights from Standard Multi-armed Bandit Experiments**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.09901) — Uses LLMs to simulate human decision-making behavior in multi-armed bandit experiments for scientific study of exploration-exploitation strategies. <sub>_Ziyuan Zhang, 2026-05-04_</sub>
- [**Persona-Grounded Safety Evaluation of AI Companions in Multi-Turn Conversations**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00227) — Uses LLM-based persona simulation to study AI companion safety risks through controlled multi-turn interactions and harm evaluation framework. <sub>_Prerna Juneja, 2026-05-04_</sub>
- [**The $\textit{Silicon Society}$ Cookbook: Design Space of LLM-based Social Simulations**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00197) — Systematically analyzes design choices in LLM-based social network simulations to study emergent behavior and model realism. <sub>_Aurélien Bück-Kaeffer, 2026-05-04_</sub>
- [**Heterogeneous Scientific Foundation Model Collaboration**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27351) — Agentic framework enabling LLM-guided multi-agent coordination across heterogeneous scientific foundation models with explicit multi-agent system design (EywaMAS, EywaOrchestra). <sub>_Zihao Li, 2026-05-01_</sub>
- [**Mapping how LLMs debate societal issues when shadowing human personality traits, sociodemographics and social media behavior**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27624) — LLMs prompted to shadow human personas and sociodemographic profiles, generating discourse for population-level behavioral analysis across controversial societal topics. <sub>_Ali Aghazadeh Ardebili, 2026-05-01_</sub>
- [**Stable Behavior, Limited Variation: Persona Validity in LLM Agents for Urban Sentiment Perception**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28048) — Paper uses LLM agents with distinct personas to simulate human perception in urban scenes, studying behavioral reproducibility and persona-induced variation in a population-scale setting. <sub>_Neemias B da Silva, 2026-05-01_</sub>
- [**The Synthetic Social Graph: Emergent Behavior in AI Agent Communities**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27271) — Comprehensive sociological study of LLM-agent populations in simulated social environment, analyzing emergent collective behavior through classical social-theory lenses. <sub>_Sungguk Cha, 2026-05-01_</sub>
- [**Can LLM Agents Simulate Multi-Turn Human Behavior? ## <a id="agent-simulation"></a>🤖 Multi-agent Systems & ABM

_Multi-agent systems, ABM, emergent behaviour, MARL, coordination._

- ⭐ [**How Much Coordination Gain Is Real? A Paired Noise-Floor Protocol for Multi-Agent LLM Benchmarks**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20695) — Empirical study of multi-agent LLM coordination mechanisms with statistical protocol for measuring real coordination gains versus noise floor. <sub>_Alibek T Kaliyev, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- ⭐ [**When Is Emergent Consensus Real? A Measured Coupling Gain and a Validity Diagnostic for LLM Agent Societies**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22203) — Empirical study of multi-agent dynamics in LLM agent societies, measuring emergent consensus and polarization behavior with methodological rigor and diagnostic validity framework. <sub>_Dongxu Yang, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Mesh Inference: A Formal Model of Collective Intelligence Without a Center**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19537) — Formal model of multi-agent collective inference where independent agents coordinate without central coordinator through local free energy relaxation. <sub>_Hongwei Xu, 2026-06-19_</sub>
- ⭐ [**LegalWorld: A Life-Cycle Interactive Environment for Legal Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18728) — Multi-stage interactive environment simulating civil litigation with multiple legal agents (lawyer, judge, litigants) interacting across causally connected stages in a procedurally faithful simulation <sub>_Songhan Zuo, 2026-06-18_</sub>

## <a id="agent-training-alignment"></a>🛡️ Alignment, Safety & Agent Training

_Training methods, benchmarks, red-teaming, interpretability, and studies of misalignment in LLMs._

- ⭐ [**Calibration Is Not Control: Why LLM-Agent Oversight Needs Intervention**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21399) — Safety-focused oversight framework for LLM agents; proposes intervention-advantage estimation to detect unrecoverable failure states and improve agent alignment via runtime control. <sub>_Chubin Zhang, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Confidence Laundering in Agent Systems: Why Uncertainty Needs a Latent Carrier**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20662) — Identifies a multi-agent system failure mode (confidence laundering) where uncertain decisions propagate without uncertainty signals, threatening alignment and safety through error amplification acros <sub>_Kaiwen Shi, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Governance Decay: How Context Compaction Silently Erases Safety Constraints in Long-Horizon LLM Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22528) — Studies a deception/specification-gaming failure mode (constraint evasion via context compaction) in long-horizon LLM agents and proposes mitigation. <sub>_Shiyang Chen, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- ⭐ [**GroundEval: A Deterministic Replacement for LLM-as-Judge in Stateful Agent Evaluation**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22737) — GroundEval is a safety/alignment diagnostic framework that detects agent failures (hallucinated evidence, temporal reasoning errors, causal mechanism violation) through grounded trajectory inspection <sub>_Jeffrey Flynt, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Group Selection Promotes Prosocial Prompts in Populations of LLM Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23343) — Multi-agent LLM population simulation studying prosocial cooperation evolution under group selection mechanisms and alignment with cooperative behaviors. <sub>_Luis Celiktemel, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Self-Improvement Can Self-Regress: The Rise-and-Collapse Failure Mode of LLM Self-Training**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21090) — Studies policy collapse during LLM self-training with RL, identifying and proposing interventions for an alignment failure mode—reward hacking leading to within-task over-optimization. <sub>_Jianzhe Lin, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Skin-Deep: A Geometric Diagnostic for Alignment Fragility in Large Language Model Representations**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22676) — Geometric diagnostic method for detecting alignment fragility and harmful-request refusal vulnerability in LLMs before deployment intervention. <sub>_Dongyub Jude Lee, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- ⭐ [**The Alignment Veto: How Safety Training Suppresses Cultural Knowledge in LLMs**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.13154) — Empirical study of alignment safety training failures (suppression vs. erasure) with interpretability analysis identifying post-training mechanisms causing safety-suppression misalignment. <sub>_Pardis Sadat Zahraei, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- ⭐ [**When Agents Commit Too Soon: Diagnosing Premature Commitment in LLM Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22936) — Interprets hidden-state signatures of behavioral failure (premature commitment) in LLM agents and develops diagnostic and monitoring methods to detect misalignment between internal state and external <sub>_Aman Mehta, 2026-06-23_</sub>
- ⭐ [**RODS: Reward-Driven Online Data Synthesis for Multi-Turn Tool-Use Agents**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19047) — Post-training method (GRPO/RL variant) addressing alignment challenge of sample efficiency in multi-turn tool-use agents via dynamic data synthesis. <sub>_Ruishan Fang, 2026-06-18_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Recursive Joint Simulation in Games**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2402.08128) — Studies multi-agent coordination through recursive joint simulation to achieve cooperation in strategic settings; directly addresses alignment of AI agent interests through game-theoretic mechanisms. <sub>_Vojtech Kovarik, 2026-06-18_</sub>
- ⭐ [**SAE Interventions are Unreliable: Post-Intervention Recovery of Suppressed Behavior**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18322) — Adversarial attack demonstrating SAE-based safety interventions can be circumvented through post-intervention recovery, revealing alignment control weaknesses. <sub>_Mingyue Cui, 2026-06-18_</sub>
- ⭐ [**The Wrong Kind of Right: Quantifying and Localizing Misfired Alignment in LLMs**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18656) — Studies a failure mode of LLM alignment where safety-oriented training overgeneralizes, causing models to reject warranted conclusions; introduces diagnostic benchmark and mechanistic analysis to dete <sub>_Naihao Deng, 2026-06-18_</sub>
- ⭐ [**In-Context Environments Induce Evaluation-Awareness in Language Models**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03824) — Adversarial attack method exposing sandbagging vulnerability in LLMs under evaluation, revealing safety-relevant misalignment mechanism and evaluation awareness. <sub>_Maheep Chaudhary, 2026-06-17_</sub>
- ⭐ [**On Surjectivity of Neural Networks: Can you elicit any behavior from your model?**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.19445) — Paper proves that modern neural architectures (transformers, diffusion models) are mathematically vulnerable to jailbreaks and can generate arbitrary outputs—a foundational safety concern for LLM-base <sub>_Haozhe Jiang, 2026-06-17_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Rift: A Conflict Signature for Deception in Language Models**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17229) — Proposes internal-activation methods to detect deceptive behavior in LLMs, addressing alignment safety by identifying when models know truth but lie—a core specification-gaming and scheming safety con <sub>_Petr Nyoma, 2026-06-17_</sub>
- ⭐ [**AgentLeak: A Benchmark for Internal-Channel Privacy Leakage in Multi-Agent LLM Systems**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.11510) — Benchmark for detecting privacy leakage and safety failures in multi-agent LLM systems—a safety diagnostic and evaluation framework revealing alignment/safety risks. <sub>_Faouzi El Yagoubi, 2026-06-16_</sub>
- ⭐ [**Constitutional Value Potentials: reading and steering internal priority margins in language models**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15420) — Interpretability method designed to detect and steer unsafe alignment behaviors—reading internal priority margins in LLMs to reveal constitutional value conflicts and violations. <sub>_Tong Che, 2026-06-16_</sub>

- [**Reward Modeling from Natural Language Human Feedback**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07349) — LLM post-training method (reward modeling for RLVR) framed explicitly around improving alignment supervision via critique-based process rewards rather than outcome-only signals. <sub>_Zongqi Wang, 2026-05-04_</sub>
- [**Stable-GFlowNet: Toward Diverse and Robust LLM Red-Teaming via Contrastive Trajectory Balance**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00553) — Red-teaming method for identifying LLM vulnerabilities and generating adversarial attacks to improve safety and alignment. <sub>_Minchan Kwon, 2026-05-04_</sub>
- [**Wasserstein Distributionally Robust Regret Optimization for Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00155) — Post-training RLHF method explicitly framed as addressing reward over-optimization (Goodharting), a known alignment failure mode where proxy rewards diverge from true objectives. <sub>_Yikai Wang, 2026-05-04_</sub>
- [**Why Do LLMs Struggle in Strategic Play? Broken Links Between Observations, Beliefs, and Actions**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00226) — Studies fundamental safety-relevant failure modes in LLM decision-making: belief-action misalignment under strategic uncertainty with interpretability analysis. <sub>_Jan Sobotka, 2026-05-04_</sub>
- [**Characterizing the Consistency of the Emergent Misalignment Persona**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28082) — Empirical study of emergent misalignment and persona consistency in fine-tuned LLMs, characterizing safety failure modes through systematic evaluation. <sub>_Anietta Weckauff, 2026-05-01_</sub>
- [**Debiasing Reward Models via Causally Motivated Inference-Time Intervention**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27495) — Proposes inference-time intervention method to debias reward models—a core component of LLM alignment—by reducing spurious feature sensitivity without capability trade-offs. <sub>_Kazutoshi Shinoda, 2026-05-01_</sub>
- [**Decoupling Reasoning and Confidence: Resurrecting Calibration in Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09117) — Post-training method (DCPO) decoupling reasoning from calibration to address over-confidence, a known LLM alignment failure mode in deployment reliability. <sub>_Zhengzhao Ma, 2026-05-01_</sub>
- [**Distributional Alignment Games for Answer-Level Fine-Tuning**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27166) — Post-training method (game-theoretic framework for answer-level fine-tuning) motivated by improving reasoning quality and alignment with answer correctness rather than reasoning traces. <sub>_Mehryar Mohri, 2026-05-01_</sub>
- [**Dynamic Adversarial Fine-Tuning Reorganizes Refusal Geometry**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27019) — Empirical mechanistic study of how adversarial fine-tuning affects refusal geometry and jailbreak robustness in safety-aligned LLMs, revealing alignment-failure dynamics. <sub>_Wenhao Lan, 2026-05-01_</sub>

- [**Let's Measure Information Step-by-Step: AI-Based Evaluation Beyond Vibes**](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.05469) — Safety-focused evaluation framework: robust mechanisms for detecting deceptive agent behavior under adversarial attack without ground truth. <sub>_Zachary Robertson, 2026-05-01_</sub>
